# Epic EHI Schema — Data Dictionary

Generated from Epic's EHI Export Specification (released **May 2026**, DocGen `su118s2p`). See the [README](../README.md) for methodology and caveats.

- **Tables:** 7,797  ·  **Columns:** 63,956  ·  **Inferred join edges:** 4,072
- **Overflow families:** 92  ·  **Org-specific columns:** 5,597 (8.8%)  ·  **Generic shared keys (unresolved):** 69
